      '\r\n' +
      'Quang Le reported that the AF_UNIX GC could garbage-collect a\r\n' +

      '\r\n' +
      'The repro consists of three stages.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  1)\r\n' +
      '    1-a. Create a single cyclic reference with many sockets\r\n' +
      '    1-b. close() all sockets\r\n' +
      '    1-c. Trigger GC\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  2)\r\n' +
      '    2-a. Pass sk-A to an embryo sk-B\r\n' +
      '    2-b. Pass sk-X to sk-X\r\n' +
      '    2-c. Trigger GC\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  3)\r\n' +
      '    3-a. accept() the embryo sk-B\r\n' +
      '    3-b. Pass sk-B to sk-C\r\n' +
      '    3-c. close() the in-flight sk-A\r\n' +
      '    3-d. Trigger GC\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'As of 2-c, sk-A and sk-X are linked to unix_unvisited_vertices,\r\n' +
      'and unix_walk_scc() groups them into two different SCCs\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  unix_sk(sk-A)->vertex->scc_index = 2 (UNIX_VERTEX_INDEX_START)\r\n' +
      '  unix_sk(sk-X)->vertex->scc_index = 3\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Once GC completes, unix_graph_grouped is set to true.\r\n' +
      "Also, unix_graph_maybe_cyclic is set to true due to sk-X's\r\n" +
      'cyclic self-reference, which makes close() trigger GC.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'At 3-b, unix_add_edge() allocates unix_sk(sk-B)->vertex and\r\n' +
      'links it to unix_unvisited_vertices.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'unix_update_graph() is called at 3-a. and 3-b., but neither\r\n' +
      'unix_graph_grouped nor unix_graph_maybe_cyclic is changed\r\n' +
      "because both sk-B's listener and sk-C are not in-flight.\r\n" +
      '\r\n' +
      "3-c decrements sk-A's file refcnt to 1.\r\n" +
      '\r\n' +
      'Since unix_graph_grouped is true at 3-d, unix_walk_scc_fast()\r\n' +
      'is finally called and iterates 3 sockets sk-A, sk-B, and sk-X\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  sk-A -> sk-B (-> sk-C)\r\n' +
      '  sk-X -> sk-X\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'This is totally fine.  All of them are not yet close()d and\r\n' +
      'should be grouped into different SCCs.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'However, unix_vertex_dead() misjudges that sk-A and sk-B are\r\n' +
      'in the same SCC and sk-A is dead.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  unix_sk(sk-A)->scc_index == unix_sk(sk-B)->scc_index -- Wrong!\r\n' +
      '  \r\n' +
      "  sk-A's file refcnt == unix_sk(sk-A)->vertex->out_degree\r\n" +
      '                                       ^-- 1 in-flight count for sk-B\r\n' +
      '  -> sk-A is dead !?\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'The problem is that unix_add_edge() does not initialise scc_index.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Stage 1) is used for heap spraying, making a newly allocated\r\n' +
      'vertex have vertex->scc_index == 2 (UNIX_VERTEX_INDEX_START)\r\n' +
      'set by unix_walk_scc() at 1-c.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      "Let's track the max SCC index from the previous unix_walk_scc()\r\n" +
      "call and assign the max + 1 to a new vertex's scc_index.\r\n" +
      '\r\n' +
      "This way, we can continue to avoid Tarjan's algorithm while\r\n" +

    title: 'CVE-2025-40215 In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'xfrm delete x->tunnel as we de...',
    link: 'https//nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2025-40215',
    pubDate: 'Thu, 04 Dec 2025 13:15:00 GMT',
    content: '![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'xfrm delete x->tunnel as we delete x\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'The ipcomp fallback tunnels currently get deleted (from the various\r\n' +
      'lists and hashtables) as the last user state that needed that fallback\r\n' +
      'is destroyed (not deleted). If a reference to that user state still\r\n' +
      'exists, the fallback state will remain on the hashtables/lists,\r\n' +
      'triggering the WARN in xfrm_state_fini. Because of those remaining\r\n' +
      'references, the fix in commit f75a2804da39 ("xfrm destroy xfrm_state\r\n' +
      'synchronously on net exit path") is not complete.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'We recently fixed one such situation in TCP due to defered freeing of\r\n' +
      'skbs (commit 9b6412e6979f ("tcp drop secpath at the same time as we\r\n' +
      'currently drop dst")). This can also happen due to IP reassembly skbs\r\n' +
      'with a secpath remain on the reassembly queue until netns\r\n' +
      "destruction. If we can't guarantee that the queues are flushed by the\r\n" +
      'time xfrm_state_fini runs, there may still be references to a (user)\r\n' +
      'xfrm_state, preventing the timely deletion of the corresponding\r\n' +
      'fallback state.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Instead of chasing each instance of skbs holding a secpath one by one,\r\n' +
      'this patch fixes the issue directly within xfrm, by deleting the\r\n' +
      'fallback state as soon as the last user state depending on it has been\r\n' +
      'deleted. Destruction will still happen when the final reference is\r\n' +
      'dropped.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'A separate lockdep class for the fallback state is required since\r\n' +
      "we're going to lock x->tunnel while x is locked. | Severity UNKNOWN  ]]>]]>]]>",
